# ER45 -- Party Chronology

Decoded from the original `chrono` table (MySQL `er45` DB, MySQL-Front dump, Windows-1250), venues resolved against the `lokacije` table. This is the live party calendar of the ER45 portal -- the backbone of the site.

## At a glance

- **3246 parties** logged (0 marked cancelled).
- **Date range:** 1991-12-26 to 2003-06-21.
- **488 distinct venues.**

**Parties per year:**

| Year | Parties |
|------|--------:|
| 1991 | 1 |
| 1992 | 2 |
| 1993 | 3 |
| 1994 | 29 |
| 1995 | 61 |
| 1996 | 56 |
| 1997 | 28 |
| 1998 | 52 |
| 1999 | 68 |
| 2000 | 105 |
| 2001 | 1110 |
| 2002 | 1556 |
| 2003 | 175 |
